 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>GOLDMAN SACHS BDC, INC. </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">200 West Street </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">New York, New
York 10282 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">May 22, 2018 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Dear Stockholder:
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">You are cordially invited to attend the 2018 Annual Meeting of Stockholders (the &#147;Meeting&#148;) of Goldman Sachs BDC, Inc. (the
&#147;Company&#148;) to be held on Friday, June&nbsp;15, 2018, at 10:00 a.m. (Eastern time), at the offices of Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P., located at 30 Hudson Street, Jersey City, New Jersey 07302. Please note that if you plan to attend
the Meeting in person, photographic identification will be required for admission. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>The Meeting is being held (i)&nbsp;to elect one
Class&nbsp;I director of the Company, who will serve until the 2021&nbsp;annual meeting of stockholders or until her successor is duly elected and qualified, (ii)&nbsp;to ratify the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP as the Company&#146;s
independent registered public accounting firm&nbsp;for the fiscal year ending December&nbsp;31, 2018 and (iii)&nbsp;to approve the application of the reduced asset coverage requirements in Section&nbsp;61(a)(2) of the Investment Company Act of 1940,
as amended, to the Company, which would permit the Company to double the maximum amount of leverage that it is permitted to incur by reducing the asset coverage requirement applicable to the Company from 200% to 150%. </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A formal Notice of Annual Meeting and Proxy Statement setting forth in detail the matters to come before the Meeting are attached hereto, and
a proxy card is enclosed for your use. You should read the Proxy Statement carefully. You will also receive separate proxy materials for the 2018 Special Meeting of Stockholders, which will be held on the same date and at the same location as the
Meeting. Please be certain to vote each proxy card that you receive from us. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>WHETHER OR NOT YOU PLAN TO BE PRESENT AT THE MEETING,
YOUR VOTE IS VERY IMPORTANT.</B> If you do not plan to be present in person at the Meeting, you can vote by signing, dating and returning the enclosed proxy card promptly or by using the Internet or telephone voting options as described on your
proxy card. If you have any questions regarding the proxy materials, please contact the Company at (800) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">621-2550.</FONT> Your prompt response will help reduce proxy costs&#151;which are paid by the Company and
indirectly by its stockholders&#151;and will also mean that you can avoid receiving <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">follow-up</FONT> phone calls and mailings. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:54%; text-indent:-2%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Sincerely, </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:54%; text-indent:-2%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">/s/ Brendan McGovern </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:54%; text-indent:-2%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Brendan McGovern </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:54%; text-indent:-2%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Chief Executive Officer and President </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>PLEASE SIGN, DATE AND RETURN THE ENCLOSED PROXY CARD IN THE ENCLOSED ENVELOPE OR USE THE INTERNET OR TELEPHONE VOTING OPTIONS TO CAST YOUR VOTE AS SOON AS
POSSIBLE. YOUR VOTE IS IMPORTANT. </B></P>

York 10282 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>NOTICE OF ANNUAL MEETING </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>To Be Held On Friday, June&nbsp;15, 2018 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">May 22, 2018 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Notice is hereby
given to the owners of shares of common stock (the &#147;Stockholders&#148;) of Goldman Sachs BDC, Inc. (the &#147;Company&#148;) that: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The 2018 Annual Meeting of Stockholders (the &#147;Meeting&#148;) will be held on Friday, June&nbsp;15, 2018, at 10:00&nbsp;a.m. (Eastern
time), at the offices of Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P. (&#147;GSAM&#148;), located at 30&nbsp;Hudson Street, Jersey City, New Jersey 07302, for the following purposes (the &#147;Proposals&#148;): </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>1.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>to elect one Class&nbsp;I director of the Company, who will serve until the 2021 annual meeting of the stockholders or until her successor is duly elected and qualified; </B></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>2.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>to ratify the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP as the Company&#146;s independent registered public accounting firm for the fiscal year ending December&nbsp;31, 2018; and </B></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>3.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>to approve the application of the reduced asset coverage requirements in Section&nbsp;61(a)(2) of the Investment Company Act of 1940, as amended, to the Company, which would permit the Company to double the maximum
amount of leverage that it is permitted to incur by reducing the asset coverage requirement applicable to the Company from 200% to 150%. </B></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The matters referred to above are discussed in the Proxy Statement attached to this Notice. On May&nbsp;1, 2018, the Board of Directors of the
Company, including each of the independent directors, unanimously recommended that you vote <B>&#147;FOR&#148;</B> each of the Proposals. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If Proposal 3 is approved by the Stockholders, the Company and GSAM intend to reduce the base management fees payable under the investment
management agreement between the Company and GSAM to annual rate of 1.00% (0.25% per quarter) of the average value of the Company&#146;s gross assets (excluding cash and cash equivalents, but including assets purchased with borrowed amounts) at the
end of each of the two most recently completed calendar quarters beginning immediately following stockholder approval. If Proposal&nbsp;3 is not approved by Stockholders, the Company will continue to operate within the 200% asset coverage
requirement until (1)&nbsp;such time as it receives Stockholder approval of a similar proposal at a future meeting or (2)&nbsp;one year after the Board of Directors approves application of the modified asset coverage requirements to the Company.
Until such time, the Company would continue to operate in accordance with its current investment strategy. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Stockholders of record at the
close of business on Thursday, May&nbsp;10, 2018 are entitled to receive notice of, and to vote at, the Meeting and at any postponements or adjournments thereof. Each Stockholder is invited to attend the Meeting in person. Please note that if you
plan to attend the Meeting in person, photographic identification will be required for admission. </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Your vote is extremely important to us. If you will not attend the Meeting in person, we urge you
to sign, date and promptly return the enclosed proxy card in the envelope provided, which is addressed for your convenience and needs no postage if mailed in the United States. You may also vote easily and quickly by Internet or by telephone. In the
event there are not sufficient votes for a quorum or to approve the Proposals at the time of the Meeting, the Meeting may be postponed or adjourned in order to permit further solicitation of proxies by the Board of Directors of the Company. </P>

instructions. Stockholders outside the United States should vote via the Internet or by submitting a proxy card instead. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">You may revoke

INC. </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">200 West Street </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">New
York, New York 10282 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>PROXY STATEMENT </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right">May 22, 2018 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This Proxy
Statement is furnished in connection with the solicitation of proxies by and on behalf of the Board of Directors (the &#147;Board&#148;) of Goldman Sachs BDC, Inc. (the &#147;Company&#148;) for use at the 2018 Annual Meeting of Stockholders (the
&#147;Meeting&#148;), to be held at the offices of Goldman Sachs Asset Management, L.P. (&#147;GSAM&#148;), located at 30 Hudson Street, Jersey City, New Jersey 07302, on Friday, June&nbsp;15, 2018, at 10:00 a.m. (Eastern time), and any postponement
or adjournment thereof. Much of the information in this Proxy Statement is required under rules of the Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#147;SEC&#148;), and some of it is technical in nature. If there is anything you do not understand,
please contact the Company at (800) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">621-2550.</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This Proxy Statement, the accompanying Notice of
Annual Meeting and proxy card and the Company&#146;s Annual Report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K</FONT> for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2017 are being mailed to stockholders (the &#147;Stockholders&#148;) of the Company of
record as of Thursday, May&nbsp;10, 2018 (the &#147;Record Date&#148;) on or about May&nbsp;24, 2018. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>PURPOSE OF THE MEETING </B></P>

would permit the Company to double the maximum amount of leverage that it is permitted to incur by reducing the asset coverage requirement applicable to the Company from 200% to 150%. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If Proposal 3 is approved by the Stockholders, the Company and GSAM intend to reduce the base management fees payable under the investment
management agreement (the &#147;Investment Management Agreement&#148;) between the Company and GSAM to an annual rate of 1.00%<B> </B>(0.25% per quarter) of the average value of the Company&#146;s gross assets (excluding cash and cash equivalents,
but including assets purchased with borrowed amounts) at the end of each of the two most recently completed calendar quarters beginning immediately following stockholder approval. If Proposal 3 is not approved by Stockholders, the Company will
continue to operate within the 200% asset coverage requirement until (1)&nbsp;such time as it receives Stockholder </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">1 </P>

approval of a similar proposal at a future meeting or (2)&nbsp;one year after the Board approves application of the modified asset coverage requirements to the Company. Until such time, the
Company would continue to operate in accordance with its current investment strategy. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>INFORMATION REGARDING THIS SOLICITATION </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">It is expected that the solicitation of proxies will be primarily by mail. The Company&#146;s officers, and personnel of the Company&#146;s
investment adviser, GSAM, and the Company&#146;s transfer agent and any authorized proxy solicitation agent, may also solicit proxies by telephone, email, facsimile, Internet or in person. If the Company records votes through the Internet or by
telephone, it will use procedures designed to authenticate Stockholders&#146; identities to allow Stockholders to authorize the voting of their shares in accordance with their instructions and to confirm that their identities have been properly
recorded. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company will pay the expenses associated with this Proxy Statement and solicitation, in a manner agreed upon by the Board.
The Company has engaged Computershare Inc. and Broadridge Financial Services, Inc. to assist in the distribution of the proxy materials and tabulation of proxies. The cost of such services with respect to the Company is estimated to be approximately
$80,000, plus reasonable <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-pocket</FONT></FONT> expenses. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">To vote
by mail, sign, date and promptly return the enclosed proxy card in the accompanying postage <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-paid</FONT> envelope. To vote by Internet or telephone, please use the control number on your proxy card and follow the
instructions as described on your proxy card. If you have any questions regarding the proxy materials, please contact the Company at (800) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">621-2550.</FONT> <B>If the enclosed proxy card is properly executed and
received prior to the Meeting and has not been revoked, the shares represented thereby will be voted in accordance with the instructions marked on the returned proxy card or, if no instructions are marked, the proxy card will be voted
&#147;FOR&#148; each of the Proposals described in this Proxy Statement; and in the discretion of the persons named as proxies in connection with any other matter that may properly come before the Meeting or any adjournment(s) or postponement(s)
thereof.</B> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Any person giving a proxy may revoke it at any time before it is exercised (1)&nbsp;by notifying the Secretary of the
Company in writing at the Company&#146;s principal executive offices, (2)&nbsp;by submitting a properly executed, later-dated proxy or (3)&nbsp;by attending the Meeting and voting in person. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If (i)&nbsp;you are a member of a household in which multiple Stockholders share the same address, (ii)&nbsp;your shares are held in
&#147;street name&#148; and (iii)&nbsp;your broker or bank has received consent to household material, then your broker or bank may send to your household only one copy of this Proxy Statement, unless your broker or bank previously received contrary
instructions from a Stockholder in your household. If you are part of a household that has received only one copy of this Proxy Statement, the Company will deliver promptly a separate copy of this Proxy Statement to you upon written or oral request.
To receive a separate copy of this Proxy Statement, please contact the Company by calling (toll-free) (800) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">621-2550</FONT> or by mail to the Company&#146;s principal executive offices at Goldman Sachs BDC, Inc., 200
West Street, New York, New York 10282.<B> </B>If your shares are held with certain banks, trust companies, brokers, dealers, investment advisers and other financial intermediaries&nbsp;(each, an &#147;Authorized Institution&#148;) and you would like
to receive a separate copy of future proxy statements, notices of internet availability of proxy materials, prospectuses or annual reports or you are now receiving multiple copies of these documents and would like to receive a single copy in the
future, please contact your Authorized Institution. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>IMPORTANT NOTICE REGARDING THE AVAILABILITY OF PROXY MATERIALS FOR THE ANNUAL

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Section&nbsp;16(a) Beneficial Ownership Reporting Compliance </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Pursuant to Section&nbsp;16(a) of the Exchange Act, the Company&#146;s directors and executive officers and any persons holding more than 10%
of the Company&#146;s common stock are required to report their beneficial ownership and any changes therein to the SEC and the Company. Specific due dates for those reports have been established, and the Company is required to report in this proxy
statement any failure to file such reports by those due dates. Based on the Company&#146;s review of Forms 3, 4 and 5 filed by such persons and information provided by the Company&#146;s directors and executive officers, the Company believes that,
with respect to the fiscal year ended December&nbsp;31, 2017, all Section&nbsp;16(a) filing requirements applicable to such persons were met in a timely manner. </P>

companies,&#148; as that term is defined in the 1940 Act.<B><SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top"> </SUP></B> </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Dollar ranges were determined using the number of shares beneficially owned as of May&nbsp;21, 2018 multiplied by the closing sales price of the Company&#146;s common stock as reported on the New York Stock Exchange
(the &#147;NYSE&#148;) on May&nbsp;21, 2018. </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">4 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>PROPOSAL 1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ELECTION OF DIRECTOR </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
Board is divided into three classes with staggered three-year terms. At each annual meeting of Stockholders, the successors to the class of directors whose term expires at such meeting will be elected to hold office for a term expiring at the annual
meeting of Stockholders held in the third year following the year of their election. At the Meeting, you will be asked to elect one Class&nbsp;I director to serve until the 2021 annual meeting of stockholders or until her successor is duly elected
and qualified or until her earlier death, resignation, removal or disqualification. In addition, the Board has adopted polices which provide that (a)&nbsp;no director shall hold office for more than 15 years and (b)&nbsp;a director shall retire as
of December 31st of the calendar year in which he or she reaches his or her 74th birthday, unless a waiver of such requirement has been adopted by a majority of the other directors.&nbsp;These policies may be changed by the directors without a
stockholder vote. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Information concerning the nominee and other relevant factors is provided below. Using the enclosed proxy card or
voting by the Internet or by telephone, a Stockholder may vote his or her shares for or against, or abstain from voting with respect to, the election of the nominee. If the enclosed proxy card is properly executed and received prior to the Meeting
(and has not been revoked) but no instructions are marked, the proxies will vote &#147;FOR&#148; the nominee. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ms.&nbsp;Susan&nbsp;B.
McGee has consented to her nomination and has agreed to serve if elected. If, at the time of the Meeting, for any reason, Ms.&nbsp;McGee is not available for election or is not able to serve as a director, the persons named as proxies intend to
exercise their voting power in favor of such person as is nominated by the Board as a substitute. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ON MAY&nbsp;1, 2018, THE BOARD,
INCLUDING EACH OF THE INDEPENDENT DIRECTORS, UNANIMOUSLY RECOMMENDED THAT YOU VOTE &#147;FOR&#148; THE NOMINEE LISTED ABOVE. </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Information about the
Nominee and Directors </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Set forth below is the name of the nominee for Class&nbsp;I director, as well as each of the continuing
directors, and their addresses, ages, terms of office, principal occupations for at least the past five years and any other directorships they hold in companies which are subject to the reporting requirements of the Exchange Act or are registered as
investment companies under the 1940 Act. Directors who (1)&nbsp;are not deemed to be &#147;interested persons,&#148; as defined in the 1940 Act, of the Company, (2)&nbsp;meet the definition of &#147;independent directors&#148; under the corporate
governance standards of the NYSE and (3)&nbsp;meet the independence requirements of Section&nbsp;10A(m)(3) of the Exchange Act are referred to as &#147;Independent Directors.&#148; Ms.&nbsp;Uniacke is deemed to be an &#147;interested person&#148; of
the Company and is referred to as the &#147;Interested Director.&#148; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Ms.&nbsp;McGee has been nominated for election as a Class&nbsp;I
director to serve until the 2021 annual meeting of stockholders. The nominee is not being proposed for election pursuant to any agreement or understanding between Ms.&nbsp;McGee and the Company. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The significance or relevance of a nominee&#146;s or director&#146;s particular experience, qualifications, attributes and/or skills is
considered by the Board on an individual basis. Experience, qualifications, attributes and/or skills common to all nominees and directors include the ability to critically review, evaluate and discuss information provided to them and to interact
effectively with the other directors and with representatives of GSAM and its affiliates, other service providers, legal counsel and the Company&#146;s independent registered public accounting firm, the capacity to address financial and legal issues
and exercise reasonable business judgment, and a commitment to the representation of the interests of the Company and the Stockholders. The Governance and Nominating Committee&#146;s charter contains certain other factors that are considered by the
Governance and Nominating Committee in identifying and evaluating potential nominees to serve as Independent Directors. Based on Ms.&nbsp;McGee&#146;s experience, qualifications, attributes and/or skills, considered individually and with respect to
the experience, qualifications, attributes and/or skills of the other directors, the Board has concluded that she should serve as, and be nominated for election by the Stockholders as, a Class&nbsp;I director. Below is a brief discussion of the
experience, qualifications, attributes and/or skills of the nominee, as well as of the continuing directors, that led the Board to conclude that such individual should serve as a director. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">8 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Class&nbsp;I Director Nominee </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Nominee for Independent Director </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Susan
B. McGee</B>. Ms.&nbsp;McGee was elected to the Board on May&nbsp;1, 2018, with such election to be effective as of June&nbsp;1, 2018. She is also expected to serve on the Board of Directors of GS PMMC. To date, Ms.&nbsp;McGee has worked for 26
years at U.S. Global Investors, Inc., an investment management firm, where she held several senior management positions, including President, General Counsel and Chief Compliance Officer. She has also been involved in the governance of the U.S.
Global Investors Funds, serving as Vice President. She plans to retire from U.S. Global Investors, Inc. and the U.S. Global Investors Funds on or about June&nbsp;1, 2018. In addition, Ms.&nbsp;McGee serves on the Board of Governors of the Investment
Company Institute and as Chairperson of the Investment Company Institute Small Funds Committee. She is also a member of the Board of Directors of the San Antonio Sports Foundation, a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">not-for-profit</FONT></FONT> organization. Based on the foregoing, Ms.&nbsp;McGee is experienced with financial and investment matters.<B> </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Continuing Directors not up for <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">re-election</FONT> at the Meeting </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Independent Directors </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Jaime
Ardila</B>. Mr.&nbsp;Ardila was elected as one of the Company&#146;s directors in February 2016 and as Chairman of the Board in January 2018. Mr.&nbsp;Ardila is retired. He also serves as director and as Chairman of the Board of Directors of GS
PMMC. Mr.&nbsp;Ardila is a member of the Board of Directors of Accenture plc, a management consulting services company, where he serves as Chair of the Finance Committee and a member of the Audit Committee, and as a member of the Board of Directors
of Ecopetrol, an integrated oil company, where he serves as Chair of the Audit Committee and a member of the Business Committee and the Corporate Governance and Sustainability Committee. Previously, Mr.&nbsp;Ardila worked for 29 years at General
Motors Company, an automobile manufacturer, where he held several senior management positions, most recently as Executive Vice President of the company and President of General Motors&#146; South America region. Mr.&nbsp;Ardila joined General Motors
in 1984. From 1996 to 1998, Mr.&nbsp;Ardila served as the managing director, Colombian Operations, of N M Rothschild&nbsp;&amp; Sons Ltd, before rejoining General Motors in 1998. Based on the foregoing, Mr.&nbsp;Ardila is experienced with financial
and investment matters.<B> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Ross J. Kari</B>. Mr.&nbsp;Kari was elected as one of the Company&#146;s directors in August 2015.
Mr.&nbsp;Kari is retired. He also serves on the Board of Directors of GS PMMC. Previously, Mr.&nbsp;Kari was Executive Vice President and Chief Financial Officer of Federal Home Loan Mortgage Corporation (Freddie Mac), where he worked for four
years. Previously, he held senior management positions at SAFECO Corporation, a personal insurance company, Federal Home Loan Bank of San Francisco, and Wells Fargo&nbsp;&amp; Company, where he began his career and worked for 19 years. Mr.&nbsp;Kari
also serves as a Director and a member of the Audit Committee and ALCO Chairman of Summit Bank. Based on the foregoing, Mr.&nbsp;Kari is experienced with financial and investment matters. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Ann B. Lane</B>. Ms.&nbsp;Lane was elected as one of the Company&#146;s directors in February 2016. Ms.&nbsp;Lane is retired. She also
serves on the Board of Directors of GS PMMC. Ms.&nbsp;Lane was a Director of Dealertrack Technologies, Inc., an automotive software solutions and services company, from 2007 to 2015. Previously, she worked for five years at JPMorgan Chase&nbsp;&amp;
Co., a financial services company, as a Managing Director and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Head</FONT> of Syndicated&nbsp;&amp; Leveraged Finance and Head of Loan Syndications Capital Markets. Prior to joining JPMorgan Chase&nbsp;&amp; Co.,
Ms.&nbsp;Lane held several senior management positions at Citigroup, Inc., a financial services company, where she worked for 18 years. Based on the foregoing, Ms.&nbsp;Lane is experienced with financial and investment matters. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">9 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>Interested Director </I></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Kaysie Uniacke</B>. Ms.&nbsp;Uniacke was elected as one of the Company&#146;s directors in January 2014. Ms.&nbsp;Uniacke is the chair of
the board of Goldman Sachs Asset Management International, serves on the boards of the Goldman Sachs Luxembourg and Dublin family of funds, several GSAM-managed pooled vehicles organized in the Cayman Islands, GS PMMC and GS MMLC and is an advisory
director to Group Inc. Previously, she was global chief operating officer of GSAM&#146;s portfolio management business until 2012 and served on the Investment Management Division Client and Business Standards Committee. Prior to this, she was
president of Goldman Sachs Trust, the GS mutual fund family, and was head of the Fiduciary Management business within Global Manager Strategies, responsible for business development and client service globally. Earlier in her career,
Ms.&nbsp;Uniacke managed GSAM&#146;s U.S. and Canadian Distribution groups. In that capacity, she was responsible for overseeing all North American institutional and third-party sales channels, marketing and client service functions, for which
client assets exceeded $200&nbsp;billion. Before that, Ms.&nbsp;Uniacke was head of GSAM&#146;s Global Cash Services business, where she was responsible for overseeing the management of assets exceeding $100&nbsp;billion. Ms.&nbsp;Uniacke worked at
Goldman Sachs from 1983 to 2012, where she was named managing director in 1997 and partner in 2002. Ms.&nbsp;Uniacke serves on the board of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Person-to-Person,</FONT></FONT> a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-profit</FONT> organization that supports the working poor in lower Fairfield County, CT. Based on the foregoing, Ms.&nbsp;Uniacke is experienced with financial and investment matters. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Compensation of Directors </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">From
January&nbsp;1, 2017 to December&nbsp;31, 2017, each Independent Director was compensated with a $130,000 annual fee for his or her services as director. In addition, the Chairman of the Board earned an annual fee of $40,000 and the director
designated as the &#147;audit committee financial expert,&#148; as defined in Item 407 of Regulation <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-K,</FONT> earned an annual fee of $10,000 for their additional services in these capacities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Effective January&nbsp;1, 2018, each of the Independent Directors receives an annual fee as compensation for his or her services as a director
of $100,000. In addition, the Chairman of the Board earns an additional annual fee of $33,000 and the director designated as the &#147;audit committee financial expert,&#148; as defined in Item 407 of Regulation
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-K,</FONT> earns an additional annual fee of $11,000 for their additional services in these capacities. The Independent Directors are reimbursed for travel and other expenses incurred in connection with attending
Board and committee meetings. The Company may also pay the incidental costs of a director to attend training or other types of conferences relating to the business development company (&#147;BDC&#148;) industry. In addition, the Company purchases
directors&#146; and officers&#146; liability insurance on behalf of the directors. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">It is the responsibility of the Independent Directors
to review their own compensation and recommend to all of the directors the appropriate level of compensation. This level of compensation may be adjusted from time to time. In conducting their review, the Independent Directors use such information as
they deem relevant, including compensation paid to directors of other BDCs of similar size and the time and effort required of the directors in fulfilling their responsibilities to the Company. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Board Composition and Leadership Structure </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company&#146;s business and affairs are managed under the direction of the Board. Pending the effectiveness of Ms.&nbsp;McGee&#146;s
election to the Board on June&nbsp;1, 2018, the Board consists of four members, three of whom are Independent Directors. The Board elects the Company&#146;s officers, who serve at the discretion of the Board. The responsibilities of the Board
include quarterly valuation of the Company&#146;s assets, corporate governance activities, oversight of the Company&#146;s financing arrangements and oversight of its investment activities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Board&#146;s role in the management of the Company is one of oversight. Oversight of the Company&#146;s investment activities extends to
oversight of the risk management processes employed by GSAM as part of its <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">day-to-day</FONT></FONT> management of the Company&#146;s investment activities. The Board reviews risk
management processes at both regular and special Board meetings throughout the year, consulting with appropriate representatives of GSAM as necessary and periodically requesting the production of risk management reports or presentations. The
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">11 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">
goal of the Board&#146;s risk oversight function is to ensure that the risks associated with the Company&#146;s investment activities are accurately identified, thoroughly investigated and
responsibly addressed. Stockholders should note, however, that the Board&#146;s oversight function cannot eliminate all risks or ensure that particular events do not adversely affect the value of the Company&#146;s investments. The Board also has
primary responsibility for the valuation of the Company&#146;s assets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Board has established an Audit Committee, Governance and
Nominating Committee, Compensation Committee, Compliance Committee and Contract Review Committee. The scope of each committee&#146;s responsibilities is discussed in greater detail below. Ms.&nbsp;McGee has been appointed to serve on each of the
above committees effective as of June&nbsp;1, 2018. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Jaime Ardila, an Independent Director, serves as Chairman of the Board. The Board
believes that it is in the best interests of the Stockholders for Mr.&nbsp;Ardila to lead the Board because of his familiarity with the Company&#146;s portfolio companies, his broad corporate background and experience with financial and investment
matters and his significant senior management experience, as described above. Mr.&nbsp;Ardila generally acts as a liaison between management, officers and attorneys between meetings of the Board and presides over all executive sessions of the
Independent Directors without management. The Board believes that its leadership structure is appropriate because the structure allocates areas of responsibility among the individual directors and the committees in a manner that enhances effective
oversight. The Board also believes that its size creates an efficient corporate governance structure that provides opportunity for direct communication and interaction between management and the Board. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Board had 10 formal meetings in 2017. Each continuing director that was a member of the Board during the fiscal year ended
December&nbsp;31, 2017 attended at least 75% of the aggregate number of meetings of the Board and of the respective committees on which he or she served. To promote effectiveness of the Board, directors are strongly encouraged to attend regularly
scheduled Board meetings in person. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">One of the Company&#146;s directors attended the 2017 Annual Meeting of Stockholders. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Committees of the Board </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Audit Committee
</I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The current members of the Audit Committee are Mr.&nbsp;Ardila, Mr.&nbsp;Kari and Ms.&nbsp;Lane, each of whom is an Independent
Director. Mr.&nbsp;Ardila simultaneously serves on the audit committees of more than three public companies, and the Board has determined that his simultaneous service on the audit committees of other public companies does not impair his ability to
effectively serve on the Audit Committee. Mr.&nbsp;Kari serves as Chairman of the Audit Committee. The Board and the Audit Committee have determined that Mr.&nbsp;Kari is an &#147;audit committee financial expert,&#148; as defined in Item 407 of
Regulation <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-K.</FONT> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit Committee is responsible for overseeing matters relating to the
appointment and activities of the Company&#146;s auditors, audit plans and procedures, various accounting and financial reporting issues and changes in accounting policies, and reviewing the results and scope of the audit and other services provided
by the independent public accountants. The Audit Committee is also responsible for aiding the Board in fair value pricing debt and equity securities that are not publicly traded or for which current market values are not readily available. The Audit
Committee&#146;s charter is available on the Company&#146;s website (<I>https://www.goldmansachsbdc.com</I>). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit Committee held
five formal meetings in 2017. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">12 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Governance and Nominating Committee </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The current members of the Governance and Nominating Committee are Mr.&nbsp;Ardila, Mr.&nbsp;Kari and Ms.&nbsp;Lane, each of whom is an
Independent Director. Mr.&nbsp;Ardila serves as the Chairman of the Governance and Nominating Committee. The Governance and Nominating Committee is responsible for identifying, researching and nominating Independent Directors for election by the
Stockholders, selecting nominees to fill vacancies on the Board or a committee of the Board, developing and recommending to the Board a set of corporate governance principles and overseeing the evaluation of the Board and management. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">All candidates nominated for an Independent Director position must meet applicable independence requirements and have the capacity to address
financial and legal issues and exercise reasonable business judgment. The Governance and Nominating Committee considers a variety of criteria in evaluating candidates (including candidates nominated by a Stockholder), including (1)&nbsp;experience
in business, financial or investment matters or in other fields of endeavor; (2)&nbsp;financial literacy and/or whether he or she is an &#147;audit committee financial expert,&#148; as defined in Item 407 of Regulation
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-K;</FONT> (3)&nbsp;reputation; (4) ability to attend scheduled Board and committee meetings; (5)&nbsp;general availability to attend to Board business on short notice; (6)&nbsp;actual or potential business, family
or other conflicts bearing on either the candidate&#146;s independence or the business of the Company; (7)&nbsp;length of potential service; (8)&nbsp;commitment to the representation of the interests of the Company and the Stockholders;
(9)&nbsp;commitment to maintaining and improving his or her skills and education; (10)&nbsp;experience in corporate governance and best business practices; and (11)&nbsp;the diversity that he or she would bring to the Board&#146;s composition. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Governance and Nominating Committee considers nominees properly recommended by a Stockholder. The Company&#146;s bylaws provide that for
any nomination to be properly brought by a Stockholder for a meeting, such Stockholder must comply with advance notice requirements and provide the Company with certain information. Generally, to be timely, a Stockholder&#146;s notice must be
received at the Company&#146;s principal executive offices not less than 90 days nor more than 120 days prior to the first anniversary date of the immediately preceding annual meeting of Stockholders. The Company&#146;s bylaws further provide that
nominations of persons for election to the Board at a special meeting may be made only by or at the direction of the Board and, provided that the Board has determined that directors will be elected at the meeting, by a Stockholder who is entitled to
vote at the meeting and who has complied with the advance notice provisions of the bylaws. The Governance and Nominating Committee&#146;s charter is available on the Company&#146;s website (<I>https://www.goldmansachsbdc.com</I>). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Governance and Nominating Committee held three formal meetings in 2017. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Compensation Committee </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
current members of the Compensation Committee are Mr.&nbsp;Ardila, Mr.&nbsp;Kari and Ms.&nbsp;Lane, each of whom is an Independent Director. The Compensation Committee is responsible for determining, or recommending to the Board for determination,
the compensation, if any, of the Company&#146;s chief executive officer and all other executive officers. The Compensation Committee also assists the Board with matters related to compensation generally, except with respect to compensation of the
directors. As discussed in &#147;Compensation of Directors,&#148; below, it is the responsibility of the Independent Directors to review their own compensation and recommend to all of the directors the appropriate level of compensation. As none of
the Company&#146;s executive officers currently is compensated by the Company, the Compensation Committee does not produce and/or review a report on executive compensation practices. The Compensation Committee&#146;s charter is available on the
Company&#146;s website (<I>https://www.goldmansachsbdc.com</I>). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Compensation Committee did not hold any formal meetings in 2017.
</P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">13 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Compliance Committee </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The current members of the Compliance Committee are Mr.&nbsp;Ardila, Mr.&nbsp;Kari and Ms.&nbsp;Lane, each of whom is an Independent Director.
Mr.&nbsp;Ardila serves as Chairman of the Compliance Committee. The Compliance Committee is responsible for overseeing the Company&#146;s compliance processes, and insofar as they relate to services provided to us, the compliance processes of the
investment adviser, underwriters (if any), administrator and transfer agent, except that compliance processes relating to the accounting and financial reporting processes and certain related matters are overseen by the Audit Committee. In addition,
the Compliance Committee provides assistance to the full Board with respect to compliance matters. The Compliance Committee&#146;s charter is available on the Company&#146;s website (<I>https://www.goldmansachsbdc.com</I>). </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Compliance Committee held five formal meetings in 2017. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Contract Review Committee </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
current members of the Contract Review Committee are Mr.&nbsp;Ardila, Mr.&nbsp;Kari and Ms.&nbsp;Lane, each of whom is an Independent Director. Mr.&nbsp;Ardila serves as Chairman of the Contract Review Committee. The Contract Review Committee is
responsible for overseeing the processes of the Board for reviewing and monitoring performance under the Company&#146;s investment management, placement agent (if any), principal underwriting (if any) and certain other agreements with GSAM and its
affiliates. The Contract Review Committee also provides appropriate assistance to the Board in connection with the Board&#146;s approval, oversight and review of the Company&#146;s other service providers, including the Company&#146;s
custodian/accounting agent, transfer agent, printing firms, and professional firms (other than the Company&#146;s independent auditor, which is the responsibility of the Audit Committee). The Contract Review Committee&#146;s charter is available on
the Company&#146;s website (<I>https://www.goldmansachsbdc.com</I>). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Contract Review Committee had one formal meeting in 2017. </P>

Alternatives portfolio management team. He is also the Chair and a voting member of the Private Credit Group&#146;s Investment Committee, which is responsible for evaluating and approving all of the Company&#146;s investments. Mr.&nbsp;McGovern
joined the firm in 2006. Prior to joining the firm, Mr.&nbsp;McGovern served as a managing director in </P>

the Global Investment Group at Amaranth Advisors, where he <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-headed</FONT> the fund&#146;s private placement efforts for both debt and equity linked products in
the United States. He is also on the board of directors for the Oxalosis and Hyperoxaluria Foundation. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Jon Yoder</B>. Mr.&nbsp;Yoder

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Jonathan Lamm</B>. Mr.&nbsp;Lamm was appointed as the Company&#146;s chief financial officer and treasurer in March 2013. Mr.&nbsp;Lamm is

infrastructure support, and IT project management, as well as the continuous improvement of the control environment. Mr.&nbsp;Lamm is secretary and a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-voting</FONT> member of the Private Credit Group&#146;s

is also the chief compliance officer of GS PMMC, GS MMLC and Goldman Sachs Trust II. Prior to joining GSAM in September 2016, she was, from November 2013 to August 2016, the General Counsel and Chief Compliance Officer of Emerging Global Advisors,
LLC (currently part of Ameriprise Financial). While at Emerging Global Advisors, Ms.&nbsp;Teufel also held the position of fund chief compliance officer from October 2015 to August 2016. Prior to joining Emerging Global Advisors, she was, from July
2005 to November 2013, Vice President, Corporate Counsel at Prudential Insurance Company of America, a subsidiary of Prudential Financial Inc., an insurance and financial services company. Prior to Prudential, Ms.&nbsp;Teufel was an associate in the

approving all of the Company&#146;s investments. Mr.&nbsp;Lentini joined the firm in 2006. Prior to joining the firm, Mr.&nbsp;Lentini was a managing director in the Global Investments Group at Amaranth Advisors, where he was responsible for trading

<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Certain Relationships and Related Party Transactions </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Investment Management Agreement </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company is party to the Investment Management Agreement, pursuant to which the Company pays GSAM, a wholly owned subsidiary of Group Inc.,
a fee for investment management services consisting of a management fee based on the Company&#146;s gross assets (excluding cash and cash equivalents but including assets purchased with borrowed amounts) and an incentive fee based on the performance
of the Company&#146;s investments. Certain of the Company&#146;s officers are also officers and employees of GSAM. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the year ended
December&nbsp;31, 2017, the Company paid GSAM a total of $28.66&nbsp;million in fees (excluding fees that are accrued but not paid) pursuant to the Investment Management Agreement, which consisted of $17.59&nbsp;million in management fees and
$11.07&nbsp;million in incentive fees. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>License Agreement </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company is party to a license agreement with an affiliate of Goldman Sachs pursuant to which the Company has been granted a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-exclusive,</FONT> royalty-free license to use the &#147;Goldman Sachs&#148; name. Under this agreement, the Company does not have a right to use the Goldman Sachs name if GSAM or another affiliate of Goldman Sachs is
not the Company&#146;s investment adviser or if the Company&#146;s continued use of such license results in a violation of applicable law, results in a regulatory burden or has adverse regulatory consequences. Other than with respect to this limited
license, the Company has no legal right to the &#147;Goldman Sachs&#148; name. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Co-Investment</FONT> Opportunities
</I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company has in the past <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-invested,</FONT> and in the future may <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-invest,</FONT> on a concurrent basis with other funds managed by GSAM and its affiliates, but not if such <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-investment</FONT> is impermissible under existing regulatory guidance,
applicable regulations or GSAM&#146;s allocation procedures. Certain types of negotiated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-investments</FONT> may be made only if the Company receives an order from the SEC permitting the Company to do so. On
January&nbsp;4, 2017, the SEC granted the Company, GS PMMC and GS MMLC, as well as certain other funds managed by GSAM in the future, the exemptive relief to make negotiated <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-investments,</FONT> subject to certain
terms and conditions in the exemptive relief. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Related Party Transaction Review Policy </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit Committee conducts quarterly reviews of any potential related party transactions brought to its attention and, during these reviews,
it also considers any conflicts of interest brought to its attention pursuant to the Company&#146;s Code of Ethics. Each of the Company&#146;s directors and executive officers is instructed and periodically reminded to inform GSAM Compliance of any
potential related party transactions. In addition, each such director and executive officer completes a questionnaire on an annual basis designed to elicit information about any potential related party transactions. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">16 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>PROPOSAL 2 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>RATIFICATION OF SELECTION OF INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">At a meeting of the Board held on December&nbsp;4, 2017, the Audit Committee selected and recommended, and the Board, including a majority of
the Independent Directors notified the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to act as the independent registered public accounting firm for the Company for the fiscal year ending December&nbsp;31, 2018. This selection is presented for
ratification by the Stockholders. If the Stockholders fail to ratify the selection of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to serve as the independent registered public accounting firm for the year ending December&nbsp;31, 2018, the Audit Committee and the
Board will reconsider the continued retention of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Representatives of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP are expected
to be present at the Meeting and will be available to respond to appropriate questions from Stockholders if necessary. Representatives of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP will be given the opportunity to make statements at the Meeting, if they so desire.
</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Audit Fees </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The aggregate
audit fees billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2017 and December&nbsp;31, 2016 were $761,500 and $570,000, respectively. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fees included in the audit fees category are those associated with the annual audits of financial statements, review of the financial
statements included in the Company&#146;s Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-Qs</FONT> and services that are normally provided in connection with statutory and regulatory filings. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Audit-Related Fees </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No
audit-related fees were billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2017 and December&nbsp;31, 2016. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Audit-related fees are for any services rendered to the Company that are reasonably related to the performance of the audits or reviews of the
Company&#146;s financial statements (but not reported as audit fees above). These services include attestation services that are not required by statute or regulation and consultations concerning financial accounting and reporting standards. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The aggregate audit-related fees billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP to GSAM, and any entity controlling, controlled by, or under common
control with, GSAM, that provides ongoing services to the Company, for engagements directly related to the Company&#146;s operations and financial reporting, for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2017 and December&nbsp;31, 2016 were $1,133,433 and
$1,157,616, respectively. These amounts represent fees PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP billed to GSAM for services related to the SSAE 16 report. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Tax
Fees </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The aggregate fees billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for services rendered to the Company for tax compliance, tax advice
and tax planning for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2017 and December&nbsp;31, 2016 were $12,500 and $12,500, respectively. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Fees
included in the tax fees category comprise all services performed by professional staff in the independent registered public accountant&#146;s tax division except those services related to the audits. This category comprises fees for tax compliance
services provided in connection with the preparation and review of the Company&#146;s tax returns. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">17 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No tax fees were billed by the Company&#146;s independent registered public accountant to GSAM,
or any entity controlling, controlled by, or under common control with, GSAM, that provides ongoing services to the Company, for engagements directly related to the Company&#146;s operations and financial reporting, for the years ended
December&nbsp;31, 2017 and December&nbsp;31, 2016. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>All Other Fees </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No fees were billed by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for products and services provided to the Company, other than the services reported in
&#147;Audit Fees,&#148; &#147;Audit Related Fees,&#148; and &#147;Tax Fees&#148; above, for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2017 and December&nbsp;31, 2016. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No other fees were billed by the Company&#146;s independent registered public accountant to GSAM, or any entity controlling, controlled by, or
under common control with, GSAM, that provides ongoing services to the Company, for engagements directly related to the Company&#146;s operations and financial reporting, for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2017 and December&nbsp;31, 2016. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Aggregate <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Audit</FONT> Fees </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">No <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> fees were billed to GSAM and service affiliates by PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP for <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2017 and December&nbsp;31, 2016. This includes any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services required to be
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approved</FONT> or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services that did not require <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> since they did not directly relate to the Company&#146;s
operations or financial reporting. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Pre-Approval</FONT> of Audit and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Audit</FONT>
Services Provided to the Company </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Audit</FONT> Services <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Pre-Approval</FONT> Policy (the &#147;Policy&#148;) adopted by the Audit Committee sets forth the procedures and the conditions pursuant to which services performed by an independent auditor for the Company may be <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approved.</FONT> Services may be <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approved</FONT> specifically by the Audit Committee as a whole or, in certain circumstances, by the Audit Committee Chairman or the person
designated as the audit committee financial expert. In addition, subject to specified cost limitations, certain services may be <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approved</FONT> under the provisions of the Policy. The Policy provides that the
Audit Committee will consider whether the services provided by an independent auditor are consistent with the SEC&#146;s rules on auditor independence. The Policy provides for periodic review and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT>
by the Audit Committee of the services that may be provided by the independent auditor. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I>De Minimis Waiver</I>. The <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> requirements of the Policy may be waived with respect to the provision of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services that are permissible for an independent auditor to perform, provided
(1)&nbsp;the aggregate amount of all such services provided constitutes no more than five percent of the total amount of revenues subject to <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> that was paid to the independent auditors during the
fiscal year in which the services are provided; (2)&nbsp;such services were not recognized by the Company at the time of the engagement to be <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services; and (3)&nbsp;such services are promptly brought
to the attention of the Audit Committee and approved prior to the completion of the audit by the Audit Committee or by one or more members of the Audit Committee to whom authority to grant such approvals has been delegated by the Audit Committee,
pursuant to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> provisions of the Policy. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><I><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Pre-Approval</FONT> of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-Audit</FONT> Services Provided to GSAM.</I>
The Policy provides that, in addition to requiring <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approval</FONT> of audit and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services provided to the Company, the Audit Committee will <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approve</FONT> those <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services provided to GSAM (and entities controlling, controlled by or under common control with GSAM that provide ongoing services to the Company)
where the engagement relates directly to the operations or financial reporting of the Company. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">18 </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit Committee has considered these fees and the nature of the services rendered, and has
concluded that they are compatible with maintaining the independence of PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP. The Audit<B> </B>Committee did not approve any of the audit-related, tax, or other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> fees described
above pursuant to the &#147;<I>de minimis</I> exceptions&#148; set forth in Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-01(c)(7)(i)(C)</FONT> and Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-01(c)(7)(ii)</FONT> of Regulation
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-X.</FONT> PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP did not provide any audit-related services, tax services or other <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services to GSAM or any entity controlling, controlled by or
under common control with GSAM that provides ongoing services to the Company that the Audit Committee was required to approve pursuant to Rule <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">2-01(c)(7)(ii)</FONT> of Regulation
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-X.</FONT> The Audit Committee considered whether the provision of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services rendered to GSAM or any entity controlling, controlled by, or under common control with
GSAM that provides ongoing services to the Company that were not <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">pre-approved</FONT> by the Audit Committee because the engagement did not relate directly to the operations and financial reporting of the Company is
compatible with maintaining PricewaterhouseCoopers LLP&#146;s independence.<B> </B> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ON MAY&nbsp;1, 2018, THE BOARD, INCLUDING EACH OF
THE INDEPENDENT DIRECTORS, UNANIMOUSLY RECOMMENDED THAT YOU VOTE &#147;FOR&#148; THE RATIFICATION OF&nbsp;PRICEWATERHOUSECOOPERS LLP AS INDEPENDENT REGISTERED PUBLIC ACCOUNTING FIRM TO THE COMPANY FOR THE FISCAL YEAR ENDING DECEMBER&nbsp;31, 2018.
</B></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">19 </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><I>Audit Committee Report</I></B> <SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:6.5pt"><B>(1)</B></FONT></SUP><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:6.5pt"> </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The following is the report of the Audit Committee of Goldman Sachs BDC, Inc. (the &#147;Company&#148;) with respect to the Company&#146;s
audited financial statements for the fiscal year ended December&nbsp;31, 2017 (the &#147;Audited Financial Statements&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit
Committee has: (a)&nbsp;reviewed and discussed the Audited Financial Statements with the management of the Company; (b)&nbsp;discussed with the independent auditor the matters required to be discussed by Auditing Standard 1301 (Communications with
Audit Committees), as adopted by the Public Company Accounting Oversight Board (&#147;PCAOB&#148;); and (c)&nbsp;received the written disclosures and the letter from the independent auditor required by applicable requirements of the PCAOB Ethics and
Independence Rule 3526 regarding the independent auditor&#146;s communications with the Audit Committee concerning independence, and has discussed with the independent auditor the auditor&#146;s independence. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The members of the Audit Committee are not, and do not represent themselves to be, professionally engaged in the practice of auditing or
accounting and are not employed by the Company for accounting, financial management or internal control purposes. Moreover, the Audit Committee relies on and makes no independent verification of the facts presented to it or representations made by
management or the Company&#146;s independent auditor. Accordingly, the Audit Committee&#146;s oversight does not provide an independent basis to determine that management has maintained appropriate accounting and/or financial reporting principles
and policies, or internal controls and procedures designed to assure compliance with accounting standards and applicable laws and regulations. Furthermore, the Audit Committee&#146;s considerations and discussions referred to above do not provide
assurance that the audit of the Company&#146;s financial statements has been carried out in accordance with the standards of the PCAOB or that the financial statements are presented in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Based on its consideration of the Audited Financial Statements and the discussions referred to above with management and the Company&#146;s
independent auditor, and subject to the limitations on the responsibilities and role of the Audit Committee set forth in the charter and those discussed above, the Audit Committee recommended to the Board of Directors that the Audited Financial
Statements be accepted by the Board of Directors and included in the Company&#146;s Annual Report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-K</FONT> for the last fiscal year for filing with the SEC. </P>
